Unified Messaging
Connect Marketing Cloud and Service Cloud Digital Engagement to messaging capabilities across email,
SMS, and third-party messaging apps such as WhatsApp. Configure these channels with your own
addresses and accounts, and then send marketing and service messages. Depending on your business
needs, you may decide to implement all channel types or just one.

=== PAGE 7 ===
Unified Messaging What’s Unified Messaging?
What’s Unified Messaging?
Learn how Unified Messaging makes it easier to message with current and potential customers from
Salesforce.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Unfied Messaging for Email and SMS is available in: Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for
Service Cloud AND Enterprise and Unlimited Editions with Marketing Cloud Next Growth and
Advanced Editions
Unified Messaging for WhatsApp is available in: Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Marketing Cloud
Engagement Growth and Advanced Editions
Not supported in Government Cloud Plus
WhatsApp Unified Messaging: Service and Marketing in One Channel
Provide your company’s service and marketing interactions in one channel built on the Unified
Conversation Platform. This unified experience makes it easy to shift between one-way marketing
promotions and two-way customer support interactions, with Data 360 powering every message. Unified
Messaging also lets you deliver personalized interactions throughout a customer’s journey using one
WhatsApp number.
Note To use an existing WhatsApp number or WhatsApp Business account in Unified Messaging,
see Number Reuse and Migration.
Email and SMS Unified Messaging: Marketing with Data 360
Unified Messaging provides the framework you need to connect your marketing activities to information
contained in Data 360. This functionality lets you store subscriber demographic and consent information
in Data 360. When the time comes to send messages or perform other marketing activities, you can use
this framework to segment and target your subscribers for meaningful interactions. This framework also
helps you maintain resources associated with your marketing activities, such as authenticated domains
for email channels and brand, campaign, and code requests for SMS channels.
SMS Unified Messaging: Service and Marketing in One Channel
Manage your company’s service and marketing interactions in one SMS channel built on the Unified
Conversation Platform. This unified experience makes it easy to shift between one-way marketing
promotions and two-way customer support interactions. Unified Messaging enables you to provide
personalized interactions throughout a customer’s journey by using one phone number.
3

=== PAGE 8 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
In SMS Unified Messaging channels, Omni-Channel determines the routing of service conversations, and
Flow handles the marketing messages. If a customer interaction is service-related, Omni-Channel routes
the message to a bot or service agent. If the interaction is marketing-related, Flow determines how to
handle the interaction. You can customize the keywords and responses associated with each use case.
SMS Unified Messaging supports text-only messages.
Important You can’t upgrade a Service Cloud Messaging channel or Marketing Cloud Engagement
channel to a Unified Messaging channel. When you set up a Unified Messaging SMS channel, use a
new phone number.
See Also
How Conversation Transitions Work in WhatsApp Unified Messaging
Set Up an SMS Unified Messaging Channel
Unified Messaging Setup
Configure each channel in the Unified Messaging section of Salesforce Setup. All channels include
required setup steps as well as optional configuration steps specific to that channel. For example, you
can enable WhatsApp for Digital Engagement and Marketing Cloud Engagement. To fully enable a
WhatsApp channel for these apps, you must both create the connection and deploy data kits and
streams for each channel in Data 360. These streams establish the relationships required to target
subscriber segments and capture data on how subscribers engage with your messages.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Unfied Messaging for Email and SMS is available in: Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for
Service Cloud AND Enterprise and Unlimited Editions with Marketing Cloud Next Growth and
Advanced Editions
Unified Messaging for WhatsApp is available in: Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Marketing Cloud
Engagement Growth and Advanced Editions
Connect to Data 360 for Unified Messaging
Before you can send messages, connect to Data 360 and deploy the required data kits. A data kit is
similar to a managed package, and it contains everything that you need to get started. Use a data kit to
create data streams, which establish the relationships that are required to track engagement and
honor consent. Create a Data 360 connection for each channel that you plan to use.
Create a Branded Domain for Unified Messaging
Use a branded domain to shorten URLs to personalized links. You can then use shortened text in your
messages and use the links to track interactions. A branded domain requires a valid CA-signed HTTPS
certificate.
Create a Unified WhatsApp Messaging Channel
Create a WhatsApp channel that supports both marketing and service interactions. Give reps access to
a full customer profile that includes both marketing and support interaction history.

consent. Create a Data 360 connection for each channel that you plan to use.

Channel Types, and Engagement Channel Types
Each unified channel type requires two data kits. One package relates to consent settings, and the other
relates to channel engagement data. You can install both at the same time, or you can install each one
separately.

Create a Branded Domain for Unified Messaging
Use a branded domain to shorten URLs to personalized links. You can then use shortened text in your
messages and use the links to track interactions. A branded domain requires a valid CA-signed HTTPS
certificate.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud AND Enterprise and Unlimited Editions
with Marketing Cloud Next Growth and Advanced Editions
Not supported in Government Cloud Plus
11.. In Setup, in the Quick Find box, search for the appropriate domain page.
aa.. For SMS domains, enter URL Shortening Domain, and then select URL Shortening Domain.
bb.. For email domains, enter Links, and then select Links in the Email section of Unified Messaging.
22.. Click New Domain.
33.. Enter the name of your domain, and select the CA-signed HTTPS certificate to use. This process
automatically adds the prefix https:// to your URL. We recommend using a subdomain for this
branded domain.
44.. Save your domain.
55.. Click the dropdown next to the domain record that you created and select Details.
66.. Configure the required DNS CNAME record with your domain registrar. Work with your IT team to
update your DNS settings and authenticate the domain.
77.. After the DNS information propagates, click Status to activate the domain.
After you activate the domain, you can select it for use when sending your messages. Shortened links
expire in 90 days and after the links expire, subscribers receive a page not found error.

Prepare for Unified WhatsApp Messaging
Before setting up a WhatsApp channel in Unified Messaging, get to know how it works. Compare
Unified Messaging channels side by side with Marketing Cloud Engagement and Service Cloud Digital
Engagement, and learn about number reuse and conversation transitions that can occur within a
WhatsApp Unified Messaging channel.
Set Up Unified WhatsApp
Unified WhatsApp setup takes place in Data Cloud, Marketing Cloud, Service Cloud and Meta. The
help docs for Unified WhatsApp setup are listed in a recommended order.
Unified WhatsApp Migration
To migrate a WhatsApp Business Account or phone number to Unified WhatsApp, follow these setup
steps.
Configure Messaging During a Support Session for Unified WhatsApp
Specify whether a message is sent to customers while they work with Service Cloud support. You can
prevent customers from receiving promotional or other low-priority content during conversations with
an agent or bot. This feature is available for only Unified WhatsApp numbers.
Unified WhatsApp Engagement Data
Use Journey Builder to transfer a WhatsApp conversation with a customer from a marketing
interaction to a service bot to give the customer additional assistance.
Pause Traffic in a WhatsApp Unified Messaging Channel
If you need to pause traffic in a Unified Messaging WhatsApp channel, temporarily disconnect the
Service Cloud Digital Engagement and Marketing Cloud Engagement apps in Setup.
Re-Register a WhatsApp Phone Number
If your WhatsApp display name is updated, a business account lock is lifted, or a channel is in an
unexpected broken state, you can re-register your WhatsApp phone number with Meta to fix it. When
you click Refresh Connection, Salesforce calls the Meta API on the already-registered number. We also
ensure that the channel is aligned and correct any missing information.
Prepare for Unified WhatsApp Messaging
Before setting up a WhatsApp channel in Unified Messaging, get to know how it works. Compare Unified
Messaging channels side by side with Marketing Cloud Engagement and Service Cloud Digital
Engagement, and learn about number reuse and conversation transitions that can occur within a
WhatsApp Unified Messaging channel.

How Conversation Transitions Work in WhatsApp Unified Messaging
With Unified Messaging, a marketing interaction and a service interaction can occur in the same
WhatsApp conversation between a customer and your business.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in:
•
Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud
•
Growth or Advanced Editions Marketing Cloud Next
•
Pro+, Corporate+, and Enterprise+ Editions for Marketing Cloud Engagement
Marketing-to-Service Transitions
Unified WhatsApp often follows a workflow in which an outbound marketing campaign is sent to a
customer. When the customer replies with anything other than a pre-defined marketing keyword that
would keep them in the campaign journey or if your org doesn't have Marketing Cloud Next set up, their
response is routed to Service Cloud for support.
What Determines a Conversation's Default Context
You control the default cloud that receives an inbound, customer-initiated Unified WhatsApp message.
We recommend using Service Cloud as the default, even if you've also connected Marketing Cloud
Engagement or Marketing Cloud Next to your Unified WhatsApp channel. Typically, an inbound,
customer-initiated message requires agent or service rep support, as opposed to being routed through a
marketing campaign. You can view your default app setting by clicking a number on the Your Numbers
page in Setup and finding the Configure Incoming Message Settings section.
15

=== PAGE 20 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
Alternatively, you can select Marketing as your default app to treat all incoming interactions as marketing
first. Incoming interactions are then routed by a marketing flow (Marketing Cloud Next) or a journey
(Marketing Cloud Engagement) if the user isn't involved in an open Service Cloud messaging session.
Learn more at Set Your Default Cloud and Routing Options for Unified WhatsApp.
Considerations for WhatsApp Unified Messaging
Review these important considerations before setting up WhatsApp Unified Messaging.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in:
•
Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud
•
Growth or Advanced Editions Marketing Cloud Next
•
Pro+, Corporate+, and Enterprise+ Editions for Marketing Cloud Engagement
•
Unified Messaging is supported in a sandbox that's created after May 9, 2025.
- Meta doesn't support business-to-business messaging.
•
We don't support associating a single WABA with more than one Salesforce org. For optimal
performance, don't reuse a WABA across multiple Salesforce orgs. A sandbox and a production org are
considered two separate orgs.
- Due to Meta's rules and regulations, some messages that you send might not be delivered to your
customers. For example, a message isn't delivered if the customer blocked your phone number,
hasn't been online for 30 days, or is in a restricted or sanctioned country. In certain situations, Meta
doesn't disclose the reason for non-delivery due to privacy and policy reasons. For more information
and potential workarounds, see WhatsApp Cloud API Support.
•
Salesforce ensures system integrity by moving messages that cannot be processed after maximum
retry attempts to a secure Dead Letter Queue (DLQ) for manual intervention and root-cause analysis.
To maintain conversational relevance and performance, any message exceeding a 24-hour processing
window will be automatically expired and purged from the queue.
Set Up Unified WhatsApp
Unified WhatsApp setup takes place in Data Cloud, Marketing Cloud, Service Cloud and Meta. The help

Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
docs for Unified WhatsApp setup are listed in a recommended order.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in:

Here are the recommended building blocks, in order, for setting up Unified WhatsApp:
11.. Data 360 lets you unify data from marketing and service clouds. Configure your Data Cloud settings
first.
22.. Tell Salesforce which WhatsApp Business Account and phone number to reference in your Unified
WhatsApp workflow.
33.. Compliance keywords.
44.. Tell Salesforce what type of Salesforce marketing system you use (Marketing Cloud Engagement or
Marketing Cloud Next), and whether you also include Service Cloud in your Unified WhatsApp setup.
Let Salesforce know which cloud's workflow to default to.
55.. Set up routing for Marketing Cloud Engagement or Marketing Cloud Next. Routing tells Salesforce
when to keep a customer in a marketing campaign or when to send them to customer support.
66.. Set up routing for Service Cloud. Choose whether to route to a user, a queue, or an Omni-Flow that
routes to a combination of agents, bots and/or users.
Configure Data Cloud for Unified WhatsApp
Data Cloud helps you store consent and engagement data for Unified WhatsApp conversations.
Connect Your WhatsApp Business Account to Salesforce for Unified WhatsApp
To use WhatsApp in Unified Messaging, connect your WhatsApp Business Account (WABA) and
number to your Salesforce account. If you don't have a WABA, we walk you through creating one.
Establish the Cross-Cloud Relationship in Unified WhatsApp
Unified WhatsApp allows outbound marketing campaigns through Marketing Cloud Next (MCN),
Marketing Cloud Engagement (MCE), or both. Unified WhatsApp allows AI agents, bots, or service reps
to field inbound messages with Service Cloud's Digital Engagement (DE). Set capabilities and a default
cloud to choose where outbound conversations originate from and how inbound conversations are
handled.
Set Your Default Cloud and Routing Options for Unified WhatsApp
Determine how incoming customer messages are directed across Marketing Cloud Engagement
(MCE), Marketing Cloud Next (MCN), and Digital Engagement (DE). We recommend that you establish
your Unified WhatsApp default app first, and then determine if custom routing logic via a marketing
journey (MCN), marketing flow (MCE), or Omni flow (DE) is necessary.
Choose Your Unified WhatsApp Data Residency
Ensure industry and regulatory compliance by selecting the country where your Unified WhatsApp
data is stored at rest. While you make your selection in Salesforce Setup, your data storage is managed
17

by Meta. This step is required for companies that comply with GDPR regulations.
Configure Marketing Cloud Next for Unified WhatsApp
Use a flow to route a customer's response to a marketing campaign. These instructions assume that
you've already activated Marketing Cloud Next and Service Cloud in your org.
Configure Marketing Cloud Engagement for Unified WhatsApp
Use a journey to route a customer's response to a marketing campaign. These instructions assume
that you've already activated Marketing Cloud Engagement and Service Cloud in your org. To enjoy the
latest marketing advancements in Salesforce, we recommend upgrading from Marketing Cloud
Engagement to Marketing Cloud Next.
Configure Service Cloud for Unified WhatsApp
Set up the Service Cloud side of Unified WhatsApp.
Configure Data Cloud for Unified WhatsApp

Unified WhatsApp allows outbound marketing campaigns through Marketing Cloud Next (MCN),

cloud to choose where outbound conversations originate from and how inbound conversations are
handled.

Set Your Default Cloud and Routing Options for Unified WhatsApp
Determine how incoming customer messages are directed across Marketing Cloud Engagement (MCE),
Marketing Cloud Next (MCN), and Digital Engagement (DE). We recommend that you establish your
Unified WhatsApp default app first, and then determine if custom routing logic via a marketing journey
(MCN), marketing flow (MCE), or Omni flow (DE) is necessary.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in:
•
Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud
22

=== PAGE 27 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
•
Growth or Advanced Editions Marketing Cloud Next
•
Pro+, Corporate+, and Enterprise+ Editions for Marketing Cloud Engagement
Your inbound routing settings consist of two main options: Setting a default app (MCE, MCN, or DE) to
receive messages, and a checkbox to prioritize marketing keywords. If Marketing Cloud Engagement is
not enabled in your org, Digital Engagement will be the only default option available, and the marketing
keyword checkbox is hidden.
Understand the Default Inbound Message Flow
When a customer sends an inbound message, the system relies on a specific hierarchy to process it,
prioritizing compliance and active conversations over default settings. Fully configured marketing flows
(MCN), marketing journeys (MCE), or Omni flows (DE) kick in after the default flow leads the customer
there.
11.. Compliance Check: The system first checks for opt-out compliance keywords. These are processed
immediately, closing out the flow. If the message contains an opt-in or help keyword, the system
checks for an active ongoing Digital Engagement conversation before processing the compliance
action. These keywords are defined in the Consent tab of the settings page for your Unified WhatsApp
number.
22.. Active Service Conversations: If the system detects an active Digital Engagement conversation, the
message routes to an agent or Service rep.
33.. Marketing Keywords: If there isn't an active service conversation, the system checks if the Allow
Marketing Cloud Engagement Reserved Keywords setting is enabled. If it is enabled and the inbound
message matches a reserved keyword set up in MCE or an active journey that applies to the user, the
response is sent to Marketing Cloud, which then handles it via a journey.
44.. Active Marketing Flows: The system then checks if MCN has an available marketing flow to resume.
55.. Default Application: If MCN isn't enabled or lacks an applicable flow, and you have MCE or DE
enabled, the message is routed to the default application you set in your configuration. The default
23

=== PAGE 28 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
setting acts as the final decision point when the system cannot find an exact action to take for a
message. If Digital Engagement is your default, an agent or Service rep conversation may start based
on your DE routing logic, and all subsequent messages enter the active conversation Omni-flow.
Set Your Default Cloud
Choose whether inbound conversations route to Service or Marketing Cloud by default. The Default App
for Incoming Messages dropdown options are based on the capability or capabilities that you configured
previously. We recommend selecting Digital Engagement as the default because inbound conversations
typically require the attention of an agent or Service rep. If MCE is enabled, additionally choose whether
marketing keywords can send customers to Marketing Cloud automatically.
11.. In Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter Your Numbers, and select Your Numbers.
22.. Under Messaging Platform Key, select the number associated with your WhatsApp Business Account.
33.. Under Process Incoming Messages, select Digital Engagement (recommended) from the Default App
for Incoming Messages dropdown field.
44.. To automatically send a conversation from Omni-Channel to Journey Builder when a marketing
keyword is sent, select Allow Marketing Cloud Engagement Reserved Keywords.
Routing Recipes for Common Customer Scenarios
Depending on your business needs and cost-sensitivity, you can configure your routing logic to support
different scenarios. These might include a scenario where marketing broadcasts outbound messages and
relies on digital engagement to handle all inbound responses. Or a scenario where you're concurrently
running MCE and MCN campaigns, and you clearly define your MCE keywords so that the system knows
how to operate. The marketing journeys, marketing flows, or Omni flows that you create beyond the
default settings help guide your unique use case.
Choose Your Unified WhatsApp Data Residency
Ensure industry and regulatory compliance by selecting the country where your Unified WhatsApp data is
stored at rest. While you make your selection in Salesforce Setup, your data storage is managed by Meta.
This step is required for companies that comply with GDPR regulations.

Unified WhatsApp Migration

Guidelines for Transferring a WhatsApp Number
To comply with Meta’s requirements and ensure a smooth migration of your WhatsApp number, follow
these guidelines.
Considerations and Limitations for Migrating a WhatsApp Business Account or Number
Before migrating your WhatsApp Business Account (WABA) or number, review these considerations
and limitations.
Migrate to Unified WhatsApp
Migrate from a business service provider, Marketing Cloud Engagement WhatsApp, or Service Cloud
WhatsApp. After migration, your existing message templates are available in Unified WhatsApp.
Add a Phone Number After WhatsApp Business Account Migration
To reduce the downtime associated with migrating a WhatsApp Business Account (WABA) and a
phone number at the same time, migrate just the WABA first. When you choose to add a phone
number later, template migration can begin within a few hours of WABA migration. If you migrate a
phone number with your WABA, template migration can take 1-2 days.
Guidelines for Transferring a WhatsApp Number
To comply with Meta’s requirements and ensure a smooth migration of your WhatsApp number, follow
these guidelines.
General Guidelines
•
To transfer your number, make sure that your account meets the customer requirements for migrating

•
When you create a messaging channel in Unified Messaging, use a new WABA.
•
To transfer a WhatsApp number from Marketing Cloud Engagement or an external service provider,
create a WABA for the number. Don’t delete the number in your existing WABA. If you delete a
number, your existing message templates aren’t migrated.
•
Before you transfer a WhatsApp number from an external service provider, make sure that your
account meets Meta’s requirements for a transfer. For more information, see WhatsApp Business
Platform: Migrate numbers among partners via Embedded Signup.
•
If you transfer a WhatsApp number from Service Cloud, you can use your existing WABA. Only WABAs
that have a history of consistently using the same phone number are eligible for migration. Before
beginning a transfer, we check to make sure that the WABA meets this requirement.
•
When you transfer a WABA from Marketing Cloud Engagement, it must have a status of Approved and
a valid payment method attached in Meta Business Manager. When you transfer a WABA, complete
these steps:
- Turn off two-step verification for the phone number.
- Use the same Meta Business Manager account that you used to set up the number.
- Use the same Meta Business Manager account that was used to set up the number. You can use the
same Business Profile Display Name for the number that you’re migrating, but specify a different
WABA name so that you can tell the accounts apart. The display name is visible to customers, but
the WABA name isn’t. You can change the display name for a phone number after the migration is
complete.
- Use a unique WABA for each Marketing Cloud Engagement business unit. Don’t share or combine
WABAs.
Considerations and Limitations for Migrating a WhatsApp Business Account or Number
Before migrating your WhatsApp Business Account (WABA) or number, review these considerations and
limitations.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in:
•
Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud
•
Growth or Advanced Editions Marketing Cloud Next
•
Pro+, Corporate+, and Enterprise+ Editions for Marketing Cloud Engagement

=== PAGE 41 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
•
To be eligible for migration, a WABA can only have one phone number associated with it, past or
present. If a second phone number was previously associated with the WABA but later deleted, the
WABA is ineligible for migration.
•
You can only migrate a WABA or phone number once. After a WABA or phone number has been
migrated from a business service provider, Marketing Cloud Engagement or Service Cloud WhatsApp
integration to Unified Messaging, it can't be used in a different Salesforce WhatsApp integration. It also
can't be migrated back to its original channel.
•
It can take up to 24 hours to migrate templates from one WhatsApp Business Account to another. For
help migrating templates before you've registered a phone number in the receiving account, open a
support case for assistance.
•
To minimize downtime that can occur during a migration, we recommend migrating your channel
during a low-traffic time.
•
When you migrate to a unified WhatsApp channel from an enhanced WhatsApp channel or
WhatsApp-First channel, your messaging history and channel settings from the previous channel are
preserved. Customers don't see any changes in their WhatsApp chat with you. If a customer messaged
with you both before and after the migration, they see all messages in the same chat.
•
If you're migrating your number from another business service provider (BSP) and can't access your
original WhatsApp Business account, ask the BSP to turn off two-step verification for your number.
Contact WhatsApp if you're not sure who your previous BSP was. If you do have access to your original
account, do it yourself.
- Log in to Meta Business Manager as an admin.
- Select your WABA and enter WhatsApp Business Manager.
- In the settings of the phone number that you're migrating, turn off two-step verification.
- Click the link in the email verification sent by WhatsApp.

Add a Phone Number After WhatsApp Business Account Migration
To reduce the downtime associated with migrating a WhatsApp Business Account (WABA) and a phone
number at the same time, migrate just the WABA first. When you choose to add a phone number later,
template migration can begin within a few hours of WABA migration. If you migrate a phone number
with your WABA, template migration can take 1-2 days.

Number of Conversations That Required an Agent or Bot Transfer
This query groups information by journey and activity details. Information returned includes a
conversation count and applicable channels. You can filter using a specified time period.
SELECT
ssot__WorkflowId__c,
COUNT(*) AS COUNT
FROM
ssot__MessageEngagement__dlm
WHERE
ssot__EngagementChannelActionId__c = 'ROUTE' AND
ssot__EngagementNotesTxt__c IN ('SERVICE_CLOUD', 'DIGITAL_MARKETING') AND
ssot__EngagementDateTm__c BETWEEN from_iso8601_timestamp('START_DATE') AND
from_iso8601_timestamp('END_DATE')

GROUP BY
ssot__WorkflowId__c
Number of Conversations That Required an Agent or Bot Transfer with
Average Transfer Time
This query groups information by journey and activity details. Information returned includes a
conversation count, journey name, activity name, and applicable channels. You can filter using a
specified time period.
SELECT
e.ssot__SendTimePhoneNumber__c AS contact,
e.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c AS transferred_event_time,
MAX(p.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c) AS transfer_event_time,
e.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c AS message_after_transfer_time,
date_diff(
'second',
MAX(p.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c),
e.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c
) AS time_difference_seconds,
e.ssot__SenderCode__c AS senderCode
FROM
ssot__MessageEngagement__dlm p
INNER JOIN ssot__MessageEngagement__dlm e ON
e.ssot__EngagementChannelActionId__c = 'ROUTE' AND
e.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c > p.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c AND
e.ssot__EngagementNotesTxt__c IN ('SERVICE_CLOUD', 'DIGITAL_MARKETING') AN
D
e.ssot__SendTimePhoneNumber__c = p.ssot__SendTimePhoneNumber__c AND
e.ssot__SenderCode__c = p.ssot__SenderCode__c
GROUP BY
e.ssot__SendTimePhoneNumber__c,
e.ssot__EngagementDateTm__c,
e.ssot__SenderCode__c

Pause Traffic in a WhatsApp Unified Messaging Channel
If you need to pause traffic in a Unified Messaging WhatsApp channel, temporarily disconnect the
Service Cloud Digital Engagement and Marketing Cloud Engagement apps in Setup.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in:
•
Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud
•
Growth or Advanced Editions Marketing Cloud Next
•
Pro+, Corporate+, and Enterprise+ Editions for Marketing Cloud Engagement
Pausing traffic can give you a chance to troubleshoot your channel configurations. You can pause all
traffic to the channel, or pause only Digital Engagement (service) or Marketing Cloud Engagement traffic.
11.. In Setup, go to the Your Numbers page under WhatsApp.
22.. Click the WhatsApp number whose traffic you want to pause.
33.. Click Disconnect next to one or both applications.
44.. Save your changes.
When traffic is paused, messages can’t be sent from or to the number in question. Agents and bots
receive errors if they try to send messages, and automated outbound messages aren’t delivered. Agents
can mark open messaging sessions inactive if you intend to resume traffic within 48 hours. The number
is still associated with your channel in Salesforce and it isn’t available for use in another channel or with a
different business service provider.
When you’re ready to resume traffic, reconnect the application or applications on the same page in
Setup. After 48 hours of traffic being paused, all open sessions are ended. If traffic is resumed before 48
hours pass, agents and bots can continue to handle their open sessions.
Re-Register a WhatsApp Phone Number
If your WhatsApp display name is updated, a business account lock is lifted, or a channel is in an
unexpected broken state, you can re-register your WhatsApp phone number with Meta to fix it. When
you click Refresh Connection, Salesforce calls the Meta API on the already-registered number. We also
ensure that the channel is aligned and correct any missing information.
53

=== PAGE 58 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
When to Re-Register Your Phone Number
Use this feature in the following scenarios:
•
Your WhatsApp display name is approved and you need the change to take effect on the channel.
•
Your WhatsApp Business account is locked and has since been unlocked by Meta.
•
Your channel is in an unexpected or broken state and standard troubleshooting has not resolved it.
Considerations for Re-Registering Your Phone Number
•
Meta enforces a limit of 10 calls per phone number within any 72-hour window. If this limit is
exceeded, Meta blocks further registration attempts for that number until the window resets. Avoid
clicking Refresh Connection repeatedly in a short period of time.
•
A verification code is not required. Unlike initial registration, re-registration does not require a new
phone verification code, as long as the number is in a connected state.
•
Clicking Refresh Connection does not interrupt or drop any conversations that are currently in
progress on the channel.
•
If you recently updated your WhatsApp display name and it has been approved by Meta, use Refresh
Connection to apply the change to your channel. The register call is only made if the new name status
is Approved and the channel is active.
Re-Register Your Phone Number
Use the Refresh Connection button to re-register your Unified WhatsApp phone number.
11.. In Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter Numbers, and then select Your Numbers.
22.. Select the Messaging Platform Key for the number that you want to re-register.
33.. Click Refresh Connection.
44.. In the confirmation dialog, review the message and click Refresh Connection.
55.. A success message confirms that the connection has been refreshed. The process takes a few minutes.

Understand Root Domains and Subdomains
A domain can include a root domain and subdomains that serve different purposes.
The root domain represents your organization’s main domain, while a sending subdomain is specifically
for sending or tracking emails. Using subdomains helps you build a sending reputation separate from
your corporate or transactional mail streams.
For example, if your From address is noreply@marketing.yourcompany.com ,
•
Root domain: yourcompany.com
•
Sending subdomain: marketing.yourcompany.com
The subdomain appears in the From address of your emails and helps ESPs or mailbox providers
associate your messages with your brand.
Set Up and Authenticate a Sending Domain
Set up and verify your sending domains in Unified Messaging to authenticate that emails originate
from your organization and not from Salesforce itself.
Functional Subdomains in Unified Messaging
After you send an email, Email Service Providers (ESPs) and subscribers communicate back to the
sender for scenarios, such as bounces, replies, or unsubscribes. To manage these inbound
communications, Unified Messaging uses functional subdomains.
CNAME Records for Functional Subdomains
To route inbound email responses correctly, each functional subdomain must have a corresponding
CNAME record in your DNS provider.
Configure CNAME Records with Your DNS Provider
To simplify setup, Unified Messaging provides the complete CNAME record names and values. You can
copy the values directly into your DNS provider’s interface.

After you send an email, Email Service Providers (ESPs) and subscribers communicate back to the sender

inbound mail types to the correct Salesforce-managed infrastructure.

Message Security
Email Service Providers (ESPs) or mailbox providers require authenticated email. Unified Messaging
provides the DNS entries that you must implement SPF, DKIM, and DMARC. These standards work
together to verify your sender identity, prevent spoofing, and improve deliverability.
DKIM CNAME Records
DomainKeys Identified Mail (DKIM) lets ESPs or mailbox providers verify that your messages are
authentic and aren't modified during delivery.
Here are Salesforce generated DKIM CNAME entries that you add to your DNS provider.
record type Name Value
CNAME s1-e360-[DKIM s1-e360-[DKIM
Key]._domainkey.marketing Key].marketing.yourcompan
.yourcompany.com y.com.dkim.[tenant].mx.sa

Key]._domainkey.marketing Key].marketing.yourcompan

lesforce.com
CNAME s3-e360-[DKIM s3-e360-[DKIM
Key]._domainkey.marketing Key].marketing.yourcompan
.yourcompany.com y.com.dkim.[tenant].mx.sa
lesforce.com
DMARC Record
DMARC (Domain-based Message Authentication, Reporting & Conformance) tells ESPs or mailbox
providers how to handle email that fails SPF or DKIM checks. Add the DMARC TXT record generated for
your domain to your DNS provider.
Note Applying a DMARC policy such as p=reject at your organizational (root) domain can affect all
corporate email sent from that domain. Misconfigured DMARC policies can cause legitimate mail to
fail. Review the configuration carefully and coordinate with your IT or network team before
enforcing a DMARC policy on your root domain.
record type Name Value
TXT _dmarc v=DMARC1; p=reject;
adkim=r; aspf=r; pct=100;

=== PAGE 65 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
See Also
Knowledge Article: Marketing Cloud Next Email Authenticated Domains Setup and DNS Tips
DNS Provider Behavior
DNS providers differ in how they handle domain naming conventions. Understanding these differences
helps prevent configuration errors.
•
DNS providers with guided experience automatically append your root domain to the CNAME Name
field. When you paste the CNAME Name, the provider may show a warning or automatically remove
your root domain from the input field. Confirm that the final saved record matches the full CNAME
Name provided by Unified Messaging.
•
Providers with verified experiences require you to enter the full name for the CNAME record but
validate it to prevent conflicts. You must enter the complete CNAME Name as provided, including all
subdomains and the root domain.
•
WYSIWYG (What You See Is What You Get) Experience providers allow any structurally correct DNS
entries. Copy and paste the full CNAME Name and Value exactly as they appear in Unified Messaging.
See Also
Knowledge Article: Marketing Cloud Next Email Authenticated Domains Setup and DNS Tips

After you add all DNS records, verify your configuration in Unified Messaging to confirm that Salesforce
recognizes and authenticates your domain. Salesforce checks the correctness of all records before
activating the domain for authenticated sending in Unified Messaging.
11.. Go to Setup > Unified Messaging > Email > Authenticated Domains.
22.. Select your domain and click Verify Domain.

Trust and Compliance in Conversational Email
Conversational Email includes controls to support user consent management and AI disclosure
requirements.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions with Marketing Cloud Next Advanced
Edition
Unsubscribe Management
Conversational Email respects subscriber communication preferences and automatically processes
unsubscribe requests.
•
Supported unsubscribe methods: All existing unsubscribe methods continue to work. Subscribers can
unsubscribe by using one-click unsubscribe links, list-header unsubscribe options, or a custom
preference center.
•
Reply-based unsubscribe: The system monitors incoming email replies for unsubscribe intent. If a
subscriber replies with an unsubscribe keyword, such as Stop or Unsubscribe, the system
automatically detects the request.
•
Impact on active conversations: When a subscriber unsubscribes through a link, preference center, or
email reply, the system removes them from the conversational flow. It then ends any active AI or
human rep conversation..
•
Communication subscriptions: When a subscriber unsubscribes, the system removes them from the
communication subscription associated with the email campaign.
•
Promotional and transactional emails: Standard unsubscribe rules apply to promotional emails. If a
transactional email has conversational capabilities enabled, a reply with an unsubscribe keyword still
73

=== PAGE 78 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
immediately ends the active conversation thread.
AI Disclosure Requirements
When an Agentforce agent generates a response, the message must include a disclosure indicating that
AI was used.
Templates that Agentforce agents use include:
•
A legal disclosure statement (for example, This message was generated using AI.)
•
An AI-specific signature identifying the agent (for example, AI Marketing Agent)
Grounded Responses
Agentforce responses are generated using approved company content, brand guidelines, and campaign
context to help ensure relevance and policy alignment.
For more information about Salesforce AI trust and data protection practices, see the Agentforce Trust
documentation.
Set Up Email Carbon Copy in Unified Messaging
Set up email carbon copy (CC) for your marketers to send copies of emails to external and internal
recipients. Both the primary recipients and the CC recipients can see who's copied on the message. Each
email sent to a CC recipient consumes a Salesforce Message Credit, in addition to credits for the primary
recipient.
RREEQQUUIIRREEDD EEDDIITTIIOONNSS
Available in: Lightning Experience
Available in: Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions with Marketing Cloud Next Growth Edition
or Advanced Edition
Not supported in Government Cloud Plus
For internal employees to receive CC emails, make sure that their email addresses are added to an
authorized email domain for your organization. If authorized domains aren’t set, then all recipients are
considered as external recipients.
You can send CC emails to these recipients.
•
External recipients: Copy stakeholders from the customer’s organization, such as an executive assistant
or other staff. In this case, the primary recipient and CC recipients are from the same organization.
•
Internal recipients: Copy team members in emails to your customers. In this case, the primary
recipient and CC recipients are from different organizations.
74

11.. From Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter Unified Messaging, and then select Send Settings.

aa.. Turn on email CC.
bb.. Set the maximum number of CC recipients from 1 through 10.
The default value is 5.
33.. Configure CC for internal recipients:
aa.. Turn on internal recipients.
bb.. Select whether to check consent for internal employees.
In Flow Builder, marketers can add CC addresses in the Send Email Message invocable action. See Send
Email Message Marketing Flow Element.
Note If the email to the primary recipient isn’t sent, for example if the primary address has a hard
bounce or lacks required consent, the CC recipients aren’t sent that message. However, if there’s a
failure while sending emails to the primary recipient at run time, CC emails are sent.

•
You can archive up to 100,000 emails per day.

•
Email attachments aren’t supported. The HTML body is stored, but attachment IDs aren’t included in

Verify Custom Fields in the Email Message Object
Email archiving doesn’t support the option to include metadata for required custom fields. Before you
turn on archiving, make sure that the Email Message object doesn’t have any custom fields set as
required.
11.. From Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter Object Manager, and then select Object Manager. Next,
click Email Message, and then scroll to the Fields & Relationships section.
22.. If the object has a custom field, click the field’s name, then click Edit.
33.. Verify that the Always require a value in this field in order to save a record checkbox isn’t selected.
If custom fields are set as required, you can’t use email archiving.
Turn On Email Archiving
11.. From Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter Email Archiving, and then select Email Archiving.
22.. Confirm that you’ve verified all requirements for email archiving.
33.. Turn on Email Archiving.
44.. Select whether users can select which emails require archiving.
After you turn on email archiving, the Archive Emails option is enabled by default in the Send Email
Message flow element.
If you turn on user control for archiving for specific sends, marketers can turn off archiving in the flow
for specific sends. However, after it's turned off, marketers can’t archive the emails from the related
campaign later. See Send Email Message Marketing Flow Element.
To view and export archived emails, set up an archive policy in the Archive app.

Email Engagement Data in Unified Messaging
Unified Messaging captures email engagement data in two data model objects (DMOs) in Data 360.
Every send or interaction with your email messaging activities generates this information. You can use
these fields to segment audiences or populate reports on your messaging activities.
EmailEngagement DMO
This DMO contains information on these email engagement event types.
•
SendStatus—the final status of a message’s delivery attempt to each recipient
•
Bounce—a sent email message couldn’t be delivered to an inbox
•
Open—an email message is opened
•
Click—a link in an email message is clicked
•
Unsubscribe—a recipient opts out of further messaging as a result of a send
•
Complaint—a recipient registers a complaint about a message with their service provider
•
Reply - recipient replies to an email message
•
Reply_conversation - recipient replies to an email message in active two way conversation
All send types include this information.
Fields Description
EventID A unique identifier for the specific event
EventType The type of event that occurred
EventDateTime A timestamp indicating when the event occurred
IndividualID A unique individual associated with the event
ContactPointEmailAddress The recipient email address used in the send
ContactPointID An identifier of the contact point record that was
used for the send
BulkEmailMessageID A unique identifier for the send entity associated
with the engagement event. Each
BulkEmailMessage in Data 360 is associated with a
ListEmail object. Context information about a
Flow Send Email action is captured to a unique
ListEmail object when the Flow is activated.
RecipientMessageID An identifier for the unique instance of a send to a
specific recipient
Component_Id An identifier for the related email component
within a dynamic content block. This value
contains the clicked link.

Sample Use Case
After the events take place, you can use the data captured to create segments for use in sending targeted
messages. For example, you can create a segment of unified individuals based on who clicked links from
your messages at least three times in the past month. Segment on the EventDateTime value associated
with the Open event types, and then collect the IndividualID values to determine who receives further
messages.
Email Send Validations in Unified Messaging
Unified Messaging automatically performs several validation checks during the email send process.
These checks help protect sender reputation, ensure compliance, and reduce the likelihood of sends
with rendering errors.
Note These validations occur only after send initiation. Sends that don't pass validation are reported
with a Not_Sent Send_Status event in the EmailEngagement DMO, along with a corresponding
engagement action reason. For more information, see Email Engagement Data in Unified
Messaging.
To make sure your sends pass the validation checks, review these recommendations.
83

=== PAGE 88 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
Platform-Managed Validations
These validations are automatically enforced on every send, regardless of the makeup of the email
content. They make sure that your email send meets system and compliance requirements.
Send validation Details
From Address Authorization
Unified Messaging verifies that the sending email
address is authorized for use. Sends from
unapproved addresses are blocked.
Not_Sent Engagement Action reason
From address not authorized to send
email.
How to pass validation
Set up and verify authenticated From Addresses to
use for your messages.
Sending Allowance Limits
Unified Messaging tracks your contractual send
allowance and stops sends that exceed your limit.
(Applicable only in Starter, Pro Suite, and
Foundations editions)
Not_Sent Engagement Action reason
Reached or exceeded sending allowance.
How to pass validation
Before executing a campaign, check Usage-Based
Entitlements in Setup (Company Information
page) for remaining available Marketing Email
Sends per Day/Month resources.
For more information, see Marketing
Considerations for Salesforce Starter and Pro Suite
Recipient Consent Status
For promotional messages, Unified Messaging
automatically suppresses sends to recipients who
haven’t provided opt-in consent to the
Communication Subscription applied to the send.
If the email isn't sent to the primary recipient, it

Content-Dependent Validations
Unified Messaging also checks for email content and data validity at send time. The success of these
validations depends on the accuracy and completeness of your content and data.
Send validation Details
Content and Personalization Rendering
Unified Messaging must be able to successfully
render the final email content for each recipient.
To optimize for recipient experience, messages
with rendering errors aren't sent.
Not_Sent Engagement Action reason
Failed to render due to syntax errors.
How to pass validation
Ensure that all personalization code is free of

syntax errors. A rendering failure will suppress the
send for the specific recipient.

Unified Messaging checks that data used for
personalization is accessible and complete. Errors
can occur if required profile attributes are missing
or if there are data source issues.
Not_Sent Engagement Action reason

How to pass validation
Ensure data graphs, profile attributes, or data
sources used for personalization are correctly set
up, and include the required, accurate data for
your intended audience.
Managed Dedicated IP Addresses
Managed dedicated IP addresses help reduce the time required to start sending email. Whether sending
your first message or scaling to larger audiences, they provide easier access to sending infrastructure that
aligns with your business needs as they grow.
As sending volume reaches predefined thresholds, Salesforce transitions your account to a dedicated
sending pool of IP addresses. This transition ensures that your infrastructure is right-sized for your current
needs and provides a dedicated route to mailbox providers.
Key benefits of managed infrastructure include:
•
Elastic resource management: The platform dynamically provisions or recovers IP addresses based on
your 30-day sending history pattern. Your infrastructure remains optimally provisioned and reduces
the need for additional purchases or manual requests.
•
Automated rebalancing: When dedicated sending is enabled, the system rebalances traffic to the new
address over a 30-day period. It incrementally shifts sending your email from the shared pool to your
dedicated pool until the transition is completed. When additional addresses are required, the system
adds them using this same process.
88

Email Sending IP Addresses
Here are the various IP statuses that explain the current state of your sending infrastructure:
IP Management Type
Type Description
General Default state. Emails are sent using Salesforce shared IP pools.
Transition A dedicated pool is created and assigned. Email traffic is gradually shifted to the
new IP addresses.
Dedicated All outbound email is sent through the dedicated IP pool linked to your account.
Pool Type
Type Description
General Shared pool of IP addresses used across all accounts within a deployment
region.
Dedicated Isolated pool of one or more IP addresses assigned to a single customer.
IP Status
Type Description
In Progress A transition period where traffic is being rebalanced from the shared pool to a
newly assigned dedicated pool.
Active The IP address is fully provisioned and actively processing your outbound email
traffic.

Manage SMS Consent in Unified Messaging
We manage consent to the SMS channel in Unified Messaging via communication subscriptions. Each
SMS code is mapped to one or more communication subscriptions. When a recipient opts in to an
SMS channel, they opt in to the communication subscriptions mapped to the SMS channel and code.
If a recipient opts out of an SMS channel, they opt out of all communication subscriptions mapped to
that SMS channel and code. Manage SMS consent and keywords for each connected number.
Set Up SMS Requirements by Country
To activate SMS sending, follow the self-service procurement process based on your country.
Request an International One-way Sending Code
Use an international one-way sending code to directly contact SMS recipients in several different
countries at the same time. Follow these instructions to request a code for use in this sending activity.
You can use the same code to send to many different countries, but each country has its own rules
and limits. Make sure that each send follows these rules.
Request a Location-Specific Sending Code
Salesforce supports SMS messaging in many countries. After you review the rules and limits for each
country that you're sending from and sending to, you can request a sender code.

You can save up to 10 drafts of your requests for brands, campaigns, and codes. Track your progress on
the Open Requests tab of the SMS Codes page, where these statuses appear.
•
Inactive: A code is available but you must provide more information before it can be activated. These
codes can't be used to send SMS messages.
•
Active: The code is available and ready to use for sending SMS messages.
•
Blocked: The code is blocked due to an expired contract or compliance violations. These codes can't
be used to send SMS messages.
•
Disabled: The code is no longer available. You can’t renew this code or use it to send SMS messages.
See Also
Sample SMS Message and Related Information for Unified Messaging
Request a Short Code for the United States and Canada
You can request a short code for sending SMS messages in the United States. Processing your short code
request can take 10–12 weeks depending on how long it takes for carriers and aggregators to provide
approval.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud AND Enterprise and Unlimited Editions
with Marketing Cloud Next Growth and Advanced Editions
Not supported in Government Cloud Plus
Before submitting the code request, you must meet these carrier audit standards to prevent multi-week
approval delays.
•
Your customer support email must use your official corporate brand domain. Don’t use generic
webmail addresses like Gmail or Yahoo.
•
SMS enrollment checkbox on your web forms must not be selected by default. Pre-checked consent
boxes result in automatic carrier rejection.
•
Web sign-up forms must explicitly include the opt-out keyword disclaimer, such as: "Reply STOP to
unsubscribe."
•
Don't use "test," "TBD," or "Toll-free" in your campaign summaries or sample copy.
11.. Before you start, verify that you have a registered brand
22.. From Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter SMS, and then select SMS Codes.
33.. Click Request Code.
44.. Select United States or Canada as the country.
55.. Select Short Code for the code type, and then click Next.
66.. To make sure that your new code is mapped to the correct app, select Marketing Cloud Edition –
Advanced/Growth or Marketing Cloud Next.
77.. Enter the brand and code and customization details.
aa.. Select your approved brand.
bb.. Enter the number of dedicated codes that you want to lease.
103

=== PAGE 108 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
cc.. Select the Search Type to find your code by a specific Number, a State, or a Zip code, or select
Random Short Code so the registry automatically assigns a sequence.
88.. Enter the basic campaign details.
aa.. Verify that Registered Brand ID is auto-populated based on the selected brand.
bb.. For Program Name, enter your public campaign name. This name must match your official
trademark or corporate DBA.
cc.. Select the Short Code Type: Vanity or Random.
dd.. For Message Cost Model, select FREE_TO_END_USER (FTEU) so subscribers aren’t charged, or
select STANDARD to apply standard carrier message and data rates.
ee.. Enter the phone number and email address for customer support contact.
99.. Define opt-in methods that your business uses to gather phone numbers and explicit consent.
aa.. Select how your customers opt in by selecting one of these options: Keyword, Web, POS, IVR, or
Other.
bb.. Enter the web address to your live corporate privacy policy and click Next.
1100.. Configure the Web Opt-In details.
aa.. For Opt-In Flow Details, describe exactly where and how a user signs up on your site. For example,
state that users opt in to receive messages through your official landing page while expressing
interest in course registration.
bb.. Specify the opt-in keywords users can text to sign up, such as JOIN or MUSIC.
cc.. Enter the call-to-action text that prompts the user.
dd.. Enter the automated opt-in success response for confirmation message.
For example, "You have successfully subscribed to updates. Messages include course reminders and
offers. Reply STOP to opt out."
1111.. Enter the mandatory keyword responses. These keywords define how subscribers can stop receiving
marketing SMS messages or get assistance.
aa.. Enter your opt-out keywords. The system defaults to standard keywords including STOP, QUIT, END,
CANCEL, and UNSUBSCRIBE.
bb.. Enter the opt-out message.
For example, "You’ve been unsubscribed from [Brand Name] alerts. You receive no further
messages. Reply START to resubscribe."
cc.. Enter the help keywords, such as Help.
dd.. Enter the help message.
For example, "For help with [Brand Name] alerts, visit [Website] or call [Phone]. Reply STOP to
unsubscribe. Message & data rates apply."
1122.. Enter compliance information.
aa.. Enter a URL for Terms & Conditions.
bb.. Enter a Privacy Policy URL.
cc.. Enter your program description summary detailing transactional alerts, onboarding assistance, or
promotional updates.
dd.. To upload supporting files such as a program syllabus, trademark certifications, or website sign up
form mockups, click Attachments.
ee.. Enter internal notes or comments detailing your consent gathering methods and opt-out
placement.
ff.. Enter a comma-separated list of collaborator email addresses to receive carrier vetting status
updates.

1144.. Submit your request.

Request an International One-way Sending Code
Use an international one-way sending code to directly contact SMS recipients in several different
countries at the same time. Follow these instructions to request a code for use in this sending activity.
You can use the same code to send to many different countries, but each country has its own rules and
limits. Make sure that each send follows these rules.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions for Service Cloud AND Enterprise and Unlimited Editions
with Marketing Cloud Next Growth and Advanced Editions
Not supported in Government Cloud Plus
11.. In Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter SMS Codes, and then select SMS Codes.
22.. Select an existing long code. If you don’t have a long code in your account yet, request a long code
(link to current process).
33.. Go to the Countries tab and click Add Countries.
44.. Select the applicable countries and click Add.
Request a Location-Specific Sending Code
Salesforce supports SMS messaging in many countries. After you review the rules and limits for each
country that you're sending from and sending to, you can request a sender code.
Available in: Lightning Experience
Salesforce Enterprise and Unlimited Editions with Marketing Cloud Next Growth or Advanced Edition
and the Salesforce Message Credits - SMS add-on
Also required: The location-specific SMS add-on for each country that you want to send to. To verify
which add-ons are available to your org, contact an account executive.

Not supported in: Government Cloud Plus
11.. Before you start, confirm that you have a registered brand and campaign.
22.. From Setup, in the Quick Find box, enter SMS, and then select SMS Codes.
33.. Click Request Code.
44.. Select the country, code type, and quantity that you want.
55.. Click Next, and continue to follow the prompts.
If you encounter an error during the request, you can enter a different code type or try the request again
after 24 hours.

Guide for Sending SMS Messages to India
109

=== PAGE 114 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
In India, the Telecom Regulatory Authority of India (TRAI) enforces strict Distributed Ledger
Technology (DLT) guidelines to combat spam messages and streamline SMS campaigns. To send SMS
messages in India, all businesses must register as a Principal Entity (PE) and get preapproval on their
headers (sender IDs) and message templates.

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Short codes are registered and applied for and approved by carriers for each campaign. Make sure you
vet your brand before a code is allocated. Short code registration is completed with a Mobile Approved
Partner. Check out the list of approved partners for CA private short code acquisition services.
•
Accenture

Capgemini

For 10DLCs, you need to request three elements:
•
Brand request—Share your company’s details and how you plan to represent your brand in your
messages.
•
Campaign request—Provide sample messages and details about your specific messaging activities.
•
Code request—Specify the nationality and type of number you want to use for sending messages.
Just like short codes, you must vet your brand before a 10DLC is allocated.
MMS Code Provisioning Guidelines for Marketing Cloud Engagement
Make sure that your Canada short code supports MMS. A short code that supports MMS automatically
includes SMS services. If you want to add MMS capability to an existing SMS short code program, you
must have a services agreement. To optimize MMS messaging, see MMS Guidelines.
Messaging Requirements
Use a call to action to engage your users. For example, send a prompt to a user to opt in to receive offers
or enter a contest.
132

=== PAGE 137 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
A call to action must include:
•
Program name
•
Message frequency
•
Link to customer terms and conditions with privacy policy and help information
Terms and conditions must include:
•
“Text STOP to stop”, including bold STOP
•
“Text HELP for help”, including bold HELP
•
A description of how the user opts in
•
How the call to action is delivered. For example: web, in-store signage
Note If you send a web form, text boxes can’t be pre-checked.
•
An opt-in keyword that, if not a web form, must be in bold
•
Screenshots of the call to action and message flow
Limitations in Unicode Support
Unicode encoding is supported for SMS messages in Canada, but there are some limitations.
•
Reduced character count—Unicode (UCS-2) encoding lets you send only 70 characters per message.
•
Concatenation impact—Multi-part Unicode messages use more segments. For example, a
160-character message is split into three parts.
•
Carrier filtering—Some CA carriers may filter, truncate, or fail to deliver messages if Unicode isn't used
properly. Unicode-heavy content might also trigger spam filters.
•
Unreliable delivery receipts—Delivery receipts may be unreliable with Unicode characters, especially
when using 10DLC or shared short codes.
Use Unicode only when necessary, such as for names or text in non-Latin scripts. Keep messages short to
avoid excessive segmentation. Avoid using emojis in critical alerts or regulatory messages. Use Unicode
carefully because of the reduced message length and potential delivery issues. For critical
communications, opt for GSM-7 encoding whenever possible.
Restricted Content
Carriers can restrict messaging with the listed content:
•
Content related to sex, hate, alcohol, firearms, and tobacco (SHAFT)
•
Content relating to illegal substances, including cannabis and cannabis-related products, such as
cannabidiol (CBD), vaping products or devices, marijuana or cannabis, or dispensaries
•
SPAM, fraud, phishing
•
Lead-generation programs
•
Deceptive programs
•
High-risk financial services, such as payday loans, short-term loans, third-party home and auto loans,
student loans, and debt collection
133

=== PAGE 138 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
•
Debt forgiveness, debt consolidation, debt reduction, and credit repair programs
•
Illegal prescriptions or drug endorsements
•
Work and investment opportunities, such as work-from-home programs, job alerts from third-party
recruiting firms, and risk investment opportunities
•
Carrier competitive promotions
•
Fraudulent or misleading messages
•
Gambling
•
Profanity
•
Depictions or endorsement of violence
•
Lead generation indicating the sharing of collected information with third parties
•
Short code programs that solicit charitable or political donations that don’t comply with Canadian
Telecommunication Association best practices.
•
Abandoned shopping cart notifications without applicable consent
•
Campaign types not in compliance with the messaging principles and best practices, Common Short
Codes Infractions Guide, and any other legal regulatory body governing telecommunication systems in
Canada
Short Code Audits
The Canadian Telecommunication Association conducts weekly short code audits to identify violations,
which include any deviations from best practice and code of conduct guidelines, such as:
•
Missing links to Terms and Conditions or Privacy Policy webpages
•
Mandatory keywords (for example, STOP and HELP) not displayed or nonfunctional
•
Failure to disclose that standard message and date rates may apply.
•
Discrepancies between the short code's current use case and its originally approved program
The timely resolution of these audits is crucial, as failure to do so can result in short code suspension.
Make sure that you maintain compliance and promptly address any audit notices.
Best Practice and Compliance References
•
WMC Global Resources for Canada
•
Mobile Marketing Association Advertising Guidelines

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Use a dedicated extended two-way short code for transaction and marketing sending. Both international
and local enterprises use this kind of code. All messages must include a preregistered tag that ranges
from 2 to 8 characters at the beginning of the message. This tag must be relevant to the enterprise or
brand sending the message. To avoid blocked sends, register all content and URLs,including shortened
URLs, before sending. Create the STOP opt-out keyword for marketing messages and include the opt-out
response 拒收请回复R at the end of the message, which directs recipients to reply with R to opt out.
Because Marketing Cloud Next doesn't permit single character keywords, inbound messages that contain
the R keyword are translated to STOP.

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Only local business entities can use an Ecuador short code for two-way sends that support marketing and
transactional sends. Otherwise, international businesses can only use an international long code for
transaction purposes, such as MFA sends, social media notifications, or international financial company
notifications. International customers sending messages that include URLs must get this content
approved and allowlisted:
•
Long code or Sender ID
•
URL
•
Message content
Network carriers require local companies maintain short code monthly sending rates of at least 100,000
sends per month to keep that code active. We recommend planning your sending rate as soon as
possible before procuring a short code. Use separate codes for marketing and transactional sending.
Conduct marketing sends from Monday through Friday, 8 AM to 6 PM (UTC−05:00). Don’t send
marketing SMS messages on weekends.
Marketing content is initially delivered from the 9107 short code to Claro numbers only. Subsequent
messages arrive from your short code. Make sure that your call-to-action messages refer to your short
code initially to make sure that your initial reply is routed correctly.
Marketing SMS messages must include the enterprise or brand name in the message body. Opt-in can
come from any channel, but you must demonstrate proof of opt-in for any complaint. STOP keywords
must be set up on the short code for processing SMS opt-out requests. Include SMS HELP keyword
messages in your program
Restricted Content

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Use a France custom alphanumeric code for one-way sending for marketing and transactional sends. You
can also use a local short code for sending. Alphanumeric codes can't be generic and must be associated
with the brand, enterprise, product, or service. These codes can only use alphanumeric characters and
spaces. Register your alphanumeric code on the French Protected Sender ID list in advance to deploy
your SMS code in this market. Confirm this registration via email or letter to ensure your sender is
protected by using Marketing Cloud Next. All letters must be printed on corporate letterhead and signed,
dated, and rubber-stamped. Incomplete or erroneous documentation causes delays in the registration
process.
You can use a two-way short code services for marketing or transactional sending, but not both. Consider
using a shared short code for marketing sends to improve time to send and cost savings. Marketing SMS
messages must include an opt-out via short code, including a call-to-action at the end of the message
such as "Nous avons recu votre demande. Vous ne devriez plus recevoir de message de notre part. SMS
non surtaxé.". Private short codes must include a contact text response such as "Service éditée par
[company name], [company address]. [company email] SMS non surtaxé opéré par [carrier]," All short
codes usage must be initiated by an MT send.
Marketing sends are banned on Sundays and public holidays. France enforces these curfews on all other
days (UTC+01:00 or +02:00, depending on the season):
•
Monday through Friday from 8 AM to 8 PM
•
Saturday from 10 AM to 6 PM

carriers must approve all alphanumeric code requests before you deploy SMS messages.
Alphanumeric codes can't be generic. They must be associated with a brand, enterprise, product, or
service. These codes can only use alphanumeric characters and spaces, with a minimum of 3 and a
maximum of 11 characters.
Restricted Content
You’re responsible for complying with local rules and regulations. To ensure compliance, familiarize
yourself with the legislation of the local market. Honduras generally forbids content related, but not
limited to, adult, politics, religious and gambling products and services.
Best Practices and Compliance References
Consider using different alphanumeric codes for marketing and transactional messaging.
Telecommunications in Honduras are regulated by the Comisión Nacional de Telecomunicaciones
(CONATEL).

In India, the Telecom Regulatory Authority of India (TRAI) enforces strict Distributed Ledger Technology

(DLT) guidelines to combat spam messages and streamline SMS campaigns. To send SMS messages in
India, all businesses must register as a Principal Entity (PE) and get preapproval on their headers (sender
IDs) and message templates.
General Guidelines and Deliverability
India is the second-largest mobile market in the world. Messaging growth continues to accelerate as rural
areas in India get mobile coverage for the first time. Approximately 40% of the population uses smart
phones. More than half of mobile devices are feature phones.

Before you send SMS messages in India, link your account to the TRAI registry.
Step 1: Register in the DLT Portal
All businesses must register as a Principal Entity on a DLT portal that is provided by an Indian telecom
operator. To complete the principal entity registration, you must provide these documents.
•
GST Certificate
•
PAN card
•
Letter of Authorization
For more information, see DLT Registration Guide.
Step 2: Register the Headers and Templates
After your principal entity is approved, register your Headers (6-character Sender IDs) and Message
Templates (message content) in the DLT portal. After your templates are approved, download them in
.csv format.
You can manage your headers and templates through one of these TRAI-authorized DLT portals.
•
ViIPower (Vodafone Idea)
•
TrueConnect (Reliance Jio)
•
Airtel DLT
•
Tata DLT
Note To avoid carrier rejection, all the variables in your templates must be tagged to
{#numeric#}, {#alphanumeric#}, or {#url#} placeholders as per the 2026 TRAI
guidelines. For more information, see the Header Verification Guide and Template Verification
Guide.
163

=== PAGE 168 ===
Unified Messaging Unified Messaging Setup
Step 3: Upload the .csv to Salesforce DLT Setup
After you download the approved .csv from the DLT portal, you must upload it to the India DLT Headers
& Templates page within Salesforce Setup. For detailed steps, see Upload DLT Headers and Templates.
Before you upload your DLT templates, keep these considerations in mind.
•
Each tenant supports only one PEID. Make sure that you enter the ID correctly; it cannot be modified
or updated after it’s saved.
•
Salesforce Setup doesn’t automatically validate your entry against the Distributed Ledger Technology
(DLT) registry. Double-check your registry details before saving.
•
When uploading data via CSV, make sure that the file contains no more than 10,000 records per
upload attempt.
•
Don’t alter the column structures or default content format of the CSV template. Editing the columns
can introduce unsupported characters, corrupting the file, and causing template validation errors.
Note To make sure the records are successfully associated with your brand's regulatory profile, your
CSV filename begins with the 19-digit Principal Entity ID (PEID). For example,
1102233445566778899_file.csv .
Compliance Requirements
For successful message delivery, adhere to these regulatory standards.
•
Achieve high message throughput (MPS) by completing the DLT registration.
•
Approvals for Principal Entity and SMS headers can take up to 4 days.
•
Every template must include a valid Consent_Type categorized as Implicit , Explicit , or
Transactional to align with recipient permissions.
•
Promotional SMS messaging is permitted only between 10:00 AM and 9:00 PM. You can send
transactional and OTP messages at any time.
•
Strict adherence to TRAI guidelines is mandatory. When you send unapproved templates or use
unregistered headers, carriers can block and fine you.
Marketing Cloud Engagement DLT Support
Marketing Cloud Engagement supports upload of DLT templates. Review these resources for more
details.
•
DLT Template Setting for SMS Messages in India
•
Use DLT Template in an SMS Message
Troubleshoot DLT Template Errors
Identify and resolve DLT template issues during the upload or activation process.

for the PEID in the India DLT Headers & Templates page.

reject special characters that aren’t UTF-8 compliant.

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Use a custom alphanumeric code with an international long code set up for one-way sending. Manage
opt-outs with a web link or customer preference center. Alphanumeric codes must be associated with
the brand, enterprise, product, or service. These codes can include only alphanumeric characters or
spaces. Codes that don't provide traffic for three months are blocked and require that you reregister the
code.
International enterprises must provide a sender ID registration form and a letter of appointment to
request their alphanumeric code. Domestic enterprises must provide 5 letters of appointment, a copy of
the company's tax ID, a copy of the company's business registration number, a screenshot and URL of
the subscriber opt-in webpage, and copies of any trademark certificates that have beenvalid for at least
one month. Financial services companies must also include a copy of their operating license from the
Ototitas Jasa Keuangan (OJK), the Indonesian financial services authority. Print all letters on corporate
letterhead, then sign, date, and rubber-stamp the copies.

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Use an Ireland alphanumeric code for one-way sends that handle both marketing and transactional
sends. Alphanumeric codes can't be generic and must be associated with the brand, enterprise, product,
or service. These codes can only use alphanumeric characters and spaces. Make sure these codes have a
minimum of 3 characters and a maximum of 11 characters. You can also use local long codes for two-
way sending for marketing and transactional sends.
Important To make sure that your SMS messages aren't labeled as “Likely Scam” or blocked, register
your alphanumeric codes in the ComReg SMS Sender ID Registry before July 2, 2025. Starting July
3, 2025, SMS messages sent from unregistered sender IDs are automatically flagged as potential
scams. From October 3, 2025, these messages are blocked and won't reach recipients. For details,
see the Implementation and Communications Plan for ComReg’s SMS Sender ID Registry and the
ComReg website.To register alphanumeric codes, follow the instructions in the SMS Sender ID
Registry Guide. During the registration process, assign Salesforce as the Third Party and authorize
Sinch Sweden AB (reference ERAU10000802) as the Originator Participating Aggregator (OPA). After
your sender IDs are approved, register them with Salesforce. Provide the list of approved sender IDs
and the Sender ID Registry Account ID for your business in the format AC: SIDR-xxxxx to your
account executive.

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Use a custom alphanumeric code with an international long code set up for one-way sending. This code
supports both marketing and transactional sends. Manage opt-outs with a web link or customer
preference center. Alphanumeric codes must be associated with the brand, enterprise, product, or
service. These codes can include only alphanumeric characters or spaces. Local carriers must approve
and allowlist all alphanumeric code requests. Use different codes for marketing and transactional sends.
Otherwise, messages and codes are blocked. Marketing alphanumeric codes begin with the prefix AD
and have a limit of 11 characters. Transactional alphanumeric codes must include 3 to 11 characters.
Local enterprises with headquarters in Kuwait must include a local trade license that's valid for at least a
month. Major brands may require additional documentation. Print all letters on corporate letterhead,
then sign, date, and rubber-stamp them.
Send marketing messages from 7 AM to 7 PM (GMT+03:00).
Restricted Content

yourself with the legislation of the local market. Failure to comply can result in service suspension,
cancellation, and potential fines. Kuwait generally forbids content related, but not limited to, these
products and services:

Adult

SMS Code Provisioning Guidelines
Use international or local long codes set up for one-way sending. Manage opt-outs with a web link or
customer preference center.
Malaysia also supports two-way marketing and transactional communication with short codes. Domestic
enterprises must register a unique alphanumeric code that's associated with their brand or enterprise.
Alphanumeric codes are used to allowlist local traffic and filter out non-registered senders. These codes
can include alphanumeric characters and spaces. Local carriers must approve and allowlist all requests
before SMS deployment. Local carriers deliver messages sent from approved alphanumeric codes using
generic local short codes.
You can procure shared short codes with up to five allocated keywords. Banks and other financial
institutions can't use shared short codes.
Begin all messages sent within Malaysia with the characters RM0. These characters count against the
total number of characters in the message, and not all carriers support concatentaion. We recommend
that you limit messages to 160 characters (70 for Unicode), including the mandatory RM0 prefix. All
messages must also include the enterprise or brand name.
Restricted Content
You’re responsible for complying with local rules and regulations. To ensure compliance, familiarize
yourself with the legislation of the local market. Failure to comply can result in service suspension,
cancellation, and potential fines. Malaysia generally forbids content related, but not limited to, these
products and services:
•
Adult
•
Alcohol
•
Gambling
•
Religion
•
Poltical
•
Tobacco
Restrict marketing communications to 8 AM to 11 PM (GMT+08:00).
